 In the final moments of the innings, Praveen Kumar (15) took some attractive shots
 tippaniyan Praveen faced two balls and hit two fours and a six
 praveen 124 ke kul yoga par ran out hue
 After this, on the very next ball, Avana caught a catch from Faulkner
 kings ilevan kii ore se trivedi, srisanth, kupar or folownar ne do-do safalataa hasil kii
 Sanju Samson's bat also made an unbeaten 27 runs
 in donon ne paanchaven wicket ke liye naabad 47 ran jode

 Bloatware means the useless apps or services that forcefully clog your phone and make your phone sluggish, breathless and slow
 sabase badi musiibat ye he ki aap inhen chaahakar bhi apane phone se hataa nahin pate
 They do not take the name of being uninstalled
 aap chaahe in Apps ko kabhi istemaal na karte hon, ye phone main pade-pade aapke phone kii memri or spes khaaenge or betry pite rahenge
 These are not Uninstall because you never downloaded them
 ye to pichley janm ke paap kii gathree kii tarah aapke phone main pehle se hi maujuud the
 When the phone company made the phone, it was handed to you by pasting the chest of software

 That is, i do not agree, i am your guest! Look into your Android phone, there will be many such garbage items that you never use, but it is not easy to get rid of
 hataae nahin hatataa phone kaa kachra -foole hue pet kii tarah, Bloatware se chhutkaaraa paane ke liye log kai upaay aajamaate hai
 If someone falls in the circle of Battery Saver and Memory Booster, then someone tries to forget those apps by removing them from the eyes
 ek tarika he aise Apps ko Disable karne kaa
 (menu> Settings> Application Manager> Go to App you want to disable> Disable)
 lekin isamen do mushkil hai

 0 yaa usase upar he
 The other problem is that many apps are not disabled in this way
 tamaam Apps aise hai jinamein Disable karne kaa Option dikhegaa hi nahin
 Another hard way to get rid of bloatware is to root the phone
 iskaa matlab he phone ke software ke bheetar ghuskar chhedchhad karnaa or apane hisaab se badlaav karnaa
 There is no use to talk about it much, because it is neither a matter of every man nor should it be done
 kyonki ek to Root karne se phone kii varantee khatm ho jaati he or agar kuch gadabad ho jaae to phone puri tarah se kharaab ho saktaa he
 Now the magic pill has come - if you want to get rid of bloatware, then without losing time, go to the Play Store and download an app called Clean Master
 ye kamaal kaa App ek nahin balki kai marjon kii dawa he
 You can guess its popularity with the fact that on the 18th of this month, the number of users using Clean Master in the world has crossed 100 million
 darasal, agar games ko chhod den to ye Play Store main sabase zyada istemaal kiye jane vaala chauthe number kaa App he
 It manufactures a company called KS Mobile, based in San Francisco, USA, which also has offices in China and Japan
 sabase badi baat ye he ki ye App ekadam muft he
 i have been using this app for a long time
 lekin aaj isaki salaah aapako dene ke peeche ek khaas vajah he
 In fact, just three days ago, this app released its version 5 with a new update
 1 laanch kiya he jiske baad ye App vaaki chamatkaarik ho gaya he

 You give it this right
 chun-chun kar karte jaao behosh -bas, ab phone se Bloatware kaa kachra saaf karnaa ekadam aasaan he
 As soon as you open Clean Master, you will see four things - Junk Files, Memory Boost, Security & Privacy and App Manager
 App Manager kaa batan dabaate hi sabase upar aapako Pre-installed apps dikh jaaenge
 And you will be really happy to see that in the list of pre-installed apps, you will see the option to disable most of the things present in the phone
 Disable karne kaa matlab he ki wo Apps phone se hate to nahin lekin yun maane kii aapane unako behosh kar diya
 Neither will they now be able to slow down your phone by running in the backgroud with their mind, nor will it blow the battery without talking nor increase the RAM or memory consumption of the phone
 ye ghar ke bekaar kachare ko baahar phenkane jaisaa he
 Now there will be more space in the house, the house will look clean and big
 intjaar kaisaa, ab aap chun-chun kar sabhi Bloatware, phaltu ke kabhi kaam na aane vaale Apps ko behoshee kii goli dete jaaen
 There will be some apps, which you have to uninstall their updates before you are disabled
 lekin ye bhi pal bhar kaa kaam he
 Just be careful, brother - but it is important to warn you here
 Clean Master ek behad powerful hathiyaar he jiskaa soch samaj kar istemaal karnaa hoga
 Do not disable the apps about which you do not understand what its work is, otherwise the phone may have problems
 haalanki galati se kuch Disable ho gaya to use dobaaraa Enable karnaa bhi itnaa hi aasaan he

 kai marjon kii ek dawa -clean Master or bhi bahut kuch karata he

 Do not get caught in it

 You will see by yourself that the phone has become faster and is running more smooth

 jaise-taise kar ke kuch hi sarkas companiyaan bachi hai jo apni bebasii or badahaali par aansu bahaane ko majaboor hai
